-- Procédures

CREATE DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` PROCEDURE `sp_update_all_salaires` ()   BEGIN
    UPDATE praticien p
    INNER JOIN grille_salariale g 
        ON p.code_type_praticien = g.code_type_praticien
        AND p.anciennete BETWEEN g.anciennete_min AND g.anciennete_max
    SET 
        p.echelon = g.echelon,
        p.salaire = g.salaire$$

--
-- Structure de la table `region`
--

CREATE TABLE `region` (
  `id` tinyint(3) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  `code` varchar(3) DEFAULT NULL,
  `nom` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `commune` varchar(4) DEFAULT NULL,
  `id_ville` mediumint(8) UNSIGNED DEFAULT NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb3 COLLATE=utf8mb3_general_ci;

--
-- Doublure de structure pour la vue `v_praticiens`
-- (Voir ci-dessous la vue réelle)
--
CREATE TABLE `v_praticiens` (
`id` int(11)
,`nom` varchar(50)
,`prenom` varchar(60)
,`date_embauche` date
,`anciennete` int(11)
,`echelon` int(11)
,`adresse` varchar(100)
,`coef_notoriete` float
,`salaire` double
,`code_type_praticien` varchar(6)
,`id_ville` mediumint(8) unsigned
,`username` varchar(50)
,`mdp` varchar(255)
,`commentaire` varchar(255)
,`anciennete_calculee` bigint(21)
);

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Structure de la vue `v_praticiens`
--
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `v_praticiens`;

CREATE ALGORITHM=UNDEFINED DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` SQL SECURITY DEFINER VIEW `v_praticiens`  AS SELECT `p`.`id` AS `id`, `p`.`nom` AS `nom`, `p`.`prenom` AS `prenom`, `p`.`date_embauche` AS `date_embauche`, `p`.`anciennete` AS `anciennete`, `p`.`echelon` AS `echelon`, `p`.`adresse` AS `adresse`, `p`.`coef_notoriete` AS `coef_notoriete`, `p`.`salaire` AS `salaire`, `p`.`code_type_praticien` AS `code_type_praticien`, `p`.`id_ville` AS `id_ville`, `p`.`username` AS `username`, `p`.`mdp` AS `mdp`, `p`.`commentaire` AS `commentaire`, timestampdiff(YEAR,`p`.`date_embauche`,curdate()) AS `anciennete_calculee` FROM `praticien` AS `p` ;
